    WHEN EXISTS (

        FROM [Clients] AS [c]
        WHERE [c].[Id] = @__clientId_0) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

2025-02-24 10:42:48.3674|INFO|Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command|Executed DbCommand (24ms) [Parameters=[@__clientId_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [o].[OrderId], [o].[ClientID], [o].[CreatedAt], [o].[TotalPrice], [c].[Id], [c].[FirstName], [c].[LastName], [t].[ProductId], [t].[OrderId], [t].[Amount], [t].[Id], [t].[Description], [t].[Name], [t].[Price]
FROM [Orders] AS [o]
INNER JOIN [Clients] AS [c] ON [o].[ClientID] = [c].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [o0].[ProductId], [o0].[OrderId], [o0].[Amount], [p].[Id], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price]
    FROM [OrderProducts] AS [o0]
    INNER JOIN [Products] AS [p] ON [o0].[ProductId] = [p].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [o].[OrderId] = [t].[OrderId]
WHERE [o].[ClientID] = @__clientId_0
